## Promotion Insights

### Color Analysis
*Statistics computed across 528 images*

| Color | Mean |
|-------|------|
| Light Blue | 31.5% |
| White | 24.5% |
| Mud Green | 24.4% |
| Gray | 23.2% |
| Blue | 21.8% |
| Black | 21.6% |
| Dark Blue | 19.8% |
| Royal Blue | 18.3% |

### Tone Distribution

| Tone | Mean |
|------|------|
| Warm | 1.9% |
| Neutral | 57.0% |
| Cool | 41.2% |
